sleipis ryse vp fra dede christ sal lychtin lycht abundant grace lyfe lycht gloir lyfe cum callit first resurrectioun ane christin man quhen grace god rysis spiritually fra ane synful lyfe ane godly verteous lyfe quhairfor writtin beatus qui habet parte resurrectione prima apoca xx happy blissit yat man woman quhilk he ony part first resurrectioun quhilk risyng fra syn mai ouir suld nocht defer spiritual resurrectioun til tyme dede mony sinful personis doi bot suld soine hastely ryse fra dede syn exempil saluiour quhilk raise tymely thrid day yi ilk ane v exhortit wisman sayand thus ne tardes conuerti ad dominum eccle v et ne differas de die diem subito enim veniet ira illius et tempore vindicte disperdet te nocht sweir lang tariand turne lord differre nocht driue nocht fra day day wrath iust iugement sal cum suddanly apon tyme vengeance distroye differre nocht thairfor thi turning god till tyme thi dede reasone gret seiknes quhairwith thow sall oppressit thow nocht haue ane cleir mynd vnderstand thai thingis quhilk belangis thi saluatioun commonly founde trew experience suppose wil nocht dispayre na mannis saluatioun mercy god reddy al tymes yit counsell sickirrar way turne god soine hastely sa lang yow differris thi conuersioun god thow tynis thi part guddis doine haly kirk thow incurris mony perrellis thi saule perseuerance syn quhair ryse vp fra dede syn soine hastely vve suld rise ane nevv lyfethridly suld ryse exempil saluiour ane new lyfe quhat new lyfe bot lyfe gydit spreit god ordourit faith hoip cheritie gud werkis procedis fra vertewis fleand fra syn occasioun syn sanct paule techis sayand thusroma vi quomodo christus surrexit mortuis per gloria patris ita et no nouitate vite ambulemus euin christ cal e fra dede glore father sa lat v gang ane new lyfe fynally saluiour ysand fra dede ane glorious lyfe eit neuir agane sa suld ryse spiritually fra ye dede syn ane new lyfe grace nocht bee agane committing dedely syn bot diligens optene ye grace god quhair throch may perseuere gud lyfe finally cum kingdome heuin quhilk grant v bocht v precious blud amen seuint artikil ix cheptour ascendit ad coelos sedet ad dextera dei patria omnipotentis beleiue saluiour ascendit heuin sittis rycht hand father god almychty yi artikil christin pepil ye may considder twa thingis first heych ascentioun christ secund profitabil v ascentioun first speikis ascendit aboue heuins spiritual say aboue ordouris angellis euin rycht hand god father almychty according sanct paule declaris sayandephe constituens iesum ad dexteram suam coelestibus super omnem principatum et potestatem et virtutem et dominationem omne nomen quod nominatur solum hoc seculo sed etiam futuro et omnia subiecit sub pedibus eius god ye father almychty he set iesus saluiour rycht hand heuinly thingis aboue principattis potestatis vertewis dominationis yat say he exaltit saluiour manheid heuinly empyre aboue nyne ordouris angellis also aboue vther creatouris may namit nocht warld bot also walrd cum powar creatouris ar subieckit subdewithovv vve suld vnderstand saluiour sittis rycht god father quhen ye say saluiour syttis rycht god father almychty think nocht yt god quhilk ane incorporal spiritual natour he oder rycht hand left hand bot rycht hand man commonly best hand sa similitude yi artikil rycht hand ye rycht syde god father best hiest maist excellent honour dignitie glore heuin quhairin god father almychty hais set saluiour aboue angellis vthir creatouris quhen speik saluiour cosidderand diuine maiestie al mekil euir hais bein euir sall secund persone ascetioun drawis hartis eftir merualously sais vbi est thesaurus tuus math ibi est cor tuum quhair thi tresour thair thi hart quhat suld tresour samekil saluiour christ quhom tresouris wisdome knawlege sa hart suld alwayis heuin according sanct paule exhortis v sayandcolos iii si consurrexistis cum christo que sursum sunt querite vbi christus est dextera dei sedens que sursu sunt sapite non finally ye may cum glorious kingdome heuin ye quhilk bring v bocht v precious blud amen aucht artikil x cheptour inde veturus est iudicare viuos mortuos beleif yt sal cu fra heuin iuge bayth quick dede pertenis ye office ane king geue sentence iugement sa wisman sais rex pro xx qui sedet solio iudicii sui dissipat omne malu intuitu suo king sittis sete iugement puttis away euil fra sycht sene coelum iesus quhilk takin vp fra yow heuin euin sa sall cum ye haue sene passand vp heuin tell v quha sal iuge general iugement lattir day quha bot saluiour iesus christ forme man sa writtinactuum x ipse est qui constitutus est deo iudex viuorum et mortuorum quhilk ordanit god iuge quick dede ye may vnderstand dede synnaris leiuand iust men wemen litterally vnderstanding dede thame quhilk he bein sall dede afore ye cuming christ iugement leiuand thame quhilk sal fonde lif cumming christ iugement quhy say ye christ sall iuge forme man trewly yat effeck yat may oppinly sein al yame quhilk sal iugit bayth gud euilioan thairfor sais self potestatem dedit ei iudiciu facere quia filius hois est god father eternal he geuin powar iesus christ mak iugement sonne quha sal iugit ye extreme iugemet doutles al men wemen quhilk he bein salbe according apostil sais cor omnes no manifestari oportet ante tribunal christi vt referat vnusquis que propria corporis prout gessit siue bonu siue malum mone euil quhairof gud sal rewardit euil sal punissit witnes haue salomonecclesi ltimo sayand thus cuncta q fiunt adducet deus iudicium pro omni errato siue bonum siue malu al thingis yat ar done god sal transitorio igne de quo dixit apstolus ipse enim saluus erit sic tamen quasi per igne non capitalia sed minuta peccata purgantur quicquid enim nobis de istis peccatis redemptu non fuerit illo igne purga dum est de quo dixit apostolus quia igne reuelabitur cuius opus arserit hoc est cremabile erit detrimentum patietur trewly sais sanct augustine transitorie fyre quhairof paule said sall saiffit
